(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the fiscal quarter ended February&#160;28, 2023 and related matters. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<IMG SRC="g488903g0328025249178.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2023 Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">Results In Line with Expectations; On Track to Full-Year Guidance </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Second quarter financial highlights and recent equity sales </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

27.2&nbsp;percent to $1.16, down 25.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting a 26&nbsp;percent headwind from lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccine and testing volumes </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

accelerating U.S. Healthcare segment sales and path to profitability </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

holdings in AmerisourceBergen and Option Care Health in the second quarter and March </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Fiscal 2023 outlook<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Maintaining full-year adjusted EPS guidance of $4.45 to $4.65 as strong core business growth is more than offset by lapping
peak <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> demand; pivoting to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-twenties</FONT> percent adjusted EPS growth in the second half of fiscal 2023 at the midpoint </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#151; March&nbsp;28, 2023 &#151; Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the second quarter of fiscal 2023,
which ended February&nbsp;28, 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Chief Executive Officer Rosalind Brewer said: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;WBA exited a solid second quarter with acceleration in February, adding to our confidence in driving strong growth in the second half of the year. With the
closing of VillageMD&#146;s acquisition of Summit Health, WBA is now one of the largest players in primary care, with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> assets across the care continuum.
Both Walgreens and Boots are performing well by delivering compelling value to consumers, playing a critical role as community health destinations, and successfully navigating a challenging environment. We will continue to take bold actions to
create sustainable long-term shareholder value.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA second quarter sales increased 3.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $34.9&nbsp;billion, an increase of
4.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income was $0.2&nbsp;billion in the second quarter compared to $1.2&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Operating income in the quarter reflects a $306&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation, Summit Health acquisition costs and
higher costs related to the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a
forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort and the Company is unable to address the probable
significance of the unavailable information. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow amounts are <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely correlated GAAP
measure </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">1 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">
Adjusted operating income was $1.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 25.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower volumes of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
vaccinations and testing lapping the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period&#146;s Omicron surge, planned payroll investments in U.S. Retail Pharmacy, and investments in U.S. Healthcare, partly offset by improved retail
contributions in the U.S., and International growth. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net earnings in the second quarter were $703&nbsp;million compared to $883&nbsp;million in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. This decrease is driven by lower operating income partially offset by a $454&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain from the partial sale of the Company&#146;s equity
method investment in AmerisourceBergen. Adjusted net earnings were $1.0&nbsp;billion, down 26.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, primarily driven by significantly lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccine and testing
volumes compared to the prior year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS in the second quarter was $0.81, compared to EPS of $1.02 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter.
Adjusted EPS decreased 27.2&nbsp;percent to $1.16, a decrease of 25.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, mainly due to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> headwind of approximately 26&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $745&nbsp;million in the second quarter. Free cash flow was $677&nbsp;million, a $7&nbsp;million increase compared with
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2023
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sales in the first six months of fiscal 2023 were
$68.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of 0.9&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, and an increase of 2.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss in the first six months of fiscal 2023 was $6.0&nbsp;billion compared to operating income of $2.5&nbsp;billion in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Operating loss in the period reflects a $6.8&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation. Adjusted operating income was
$2.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 34.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> headwind of approximately 24&nbsp;percent, planned payroll and IT investments in U.S. Retail Pharmacy and
growth investments in U.S. Healthcare, partly offset by improved retail contributions in the U.S., and International growth. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the first six months of fiscal
2023, net loss was $3.0&nbsp;billion compared to net earnings of $4.5&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. This decrease is driven by a $5.4&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT>
charge for opioid-related claims and litigation offset by a $1.4&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain from the partial sale of the Company&#146;s equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen, and lapping a
$2.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain on the Company&#146;s investments in VillageMD and Shields Health Solutions in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted net earnings were
$2.0&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 28.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, primarily driven by lower adjusted operating income. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Loss per share for the first
six months of fiscal<B> </B>2023<B> </B>was $3.50 compared to EPS of $5.15 from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted EPS decreased 29.0&nbsp;percent to $2.32, reflecting a decrease of 27.9&nbsp;percent on a constant
currency basis, mainly due to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> headwind of approximately 22&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating
activities was $1.2&nbsp;billion in the first six months of fiscal 2023, a decrease of $0.9&nbsp;billion from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, and free cash flow was $560&nbsp;million, a decrease of $754&nbsp;million from
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period driven by lower earnings and increased capital expenditures in growth initiatives, partially offset by ongoing working capital optimization. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">2 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA
continues to achieve strong results across its business and strategic priorities, including: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Transform and align the core </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="11%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Launched FY22 <U>Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) Report</U> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Included as part of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI) for the third consecutive year, scoring in the 87th
percentile within the Food&nbsp;&amp; Staples Retailing industry group </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Segments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>U.S. Retail Pharmacy: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment had second quarter
sales of $27.6&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 0.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable sales increased 3.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter while
lapping strong comparable sales growth of 9.5&nbsp;percent in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, which included a significant contribution from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmacy sales increased 0.3&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, negatively impacted by a 3.5 percentage point
headwind from AllianceRx Walgreens. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 4.9&nbsp;percent in the quarter, benefiting from branded drug inflation. Comparable prescriptions filled in the quarter increased 0.2&nbsp;percent, while comparable
prescriptions excluding immunizations increased 3.5&nbsp;percent, a sequential improvement of 140 basis points compared to the prior quarter. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents, decreased 0.7&nbsp;percent to 298.0&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales decreased 1.8&nbsp;percent and comparable
retail sales decreased 1.0&nbsp;percent in the second quarter compared to comparable sales growth of 14.7&nbsp;percent in the prior year quarter. Excluding tobacco, comparable retail sales decreased 0.5&nbsp;percent including a 500 basis point
headwind from lower sales of OTC test kits, partly offset by strong core growth across all categories. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">3 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 10.2&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter.
Adjusted gross profit decreased 9.8&nbsp;percent. Gross profit and adjusted gross profit were entirely driven by a 10 percentage point headwind from lower contributions from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing.
Reimbursement net of procurement savings was offset by higher retail gross profit from gross margin expansion and strong underlying sales performance across categories. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Selling, general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A) increased 6.3&nbsp;percent to $5.5&nbsp;billion, including a $306&nbsp;million
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation in the current quarter. Adjusted SG&amp;A decreased 3.2&nbsp;percent to $4.9&nbsp;billion, driven by reduced labor for lower volumes of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing and savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program, partly offset by increased labor investments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the second quarter was $0.4&nbsp;billion compared to operating income of $1.4&nbsp;billion from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, reflecting the $306&nbsp;million charge related to opioid claims and litigation in the current quarter. Adjusted operating income decreased 32.8&nbsp;percent to $1.1&nbsp;billion from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, reflecting a 29 percentage point headwind from lower contributions of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing, continued reimbursement pressure net of procurement, and planned labor investments. These
impacts were partly offset by improved retail gross profit, driven by gross margin expansion and strong underlying sales performance across categories. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The International segment had second quarter sales of
$5.7&nbsp;billion, an increase of 1.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, held back by an adverse currency impact of 7.5 percentage points. Sales increased 9.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis,
with Boots UK sales growing 11.0&nbsp;percent, and the Germany wholesale business growing 7.5&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased
2.0&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter held back by lower demand for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> services. Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 16.0&nbsp;percent
compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, growing market share for the eighth consecutive quarter. Footfall improved by 16&nbsp;percent, compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter.
Boots.com continued to perform well, accounting for over 15&nbsp;percent of retail sales in the quarter compared to approximately 9&nbsp;percent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 0.7&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 8.2
percentage points. Gross profit increased 7.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting higher UK retail sales and solid execution in the Germany wholesale business, partly offset by lower demand for
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related services in the UK and the adverse gross margin impact of National Health Service pharmacy funding. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A in the quarter decreased 18.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $846&nbsp;million, including a favorable
currency impact of 7.6 percentage points, and lower acquisition related costs. Adjusted SG&amp;A decreased 5.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting real estate gains from the company&#146;s cash mobilization program in Germany, and
effective cost management, partly offset in the UK by increased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-store</FONT> and marketing activities, higher inflation, and lapping temporary <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related benefits in
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income increased 104.0&nbsp;percent from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $353&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating income increased 55.8&nbsp;percent to $352&nbsp;million, an increase of 65.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>U.S. Healthcare: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The U.S. Healthcare segment had second quarter sales of
$1.6&nbsp;billion, an increase of $1.1&nbsp;billion compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. On a pro forma basis, the segment&#146;s businesses grew sales at a combined rate of 30&nbsp;percent in the quarter.
VillageMD, including Summit Health, grew pro forma sales 30&nbsp;percent, reflecting existing clinic growth, and clinic footprint expansion. Shields grew pro forma sales 41&nbsp;percent, driven by recent contract wins, further expansion of existing
partnerships, and strong executional focus. CareCentrix grew pro forma sales 25&nbsp;percent as a result of additional service offerings with existing partners. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">4 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit was $32&nbsp;million as Shields and CareCentrix gross profit was more than offset by VillageMD&#146;s
expansion. VillageMD added 133 clinics compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted gross profit was $110&nbsp;million, an increase of $95&nbsp;million compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period as the segment continues to rapidly scale. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Second quarter SG&amp;A was $504&nbsp;million, and adjusted
SG&amp;A was $269&nbsp;million. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased by $177&nbsp;million compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, primarily due to the acquisitions of CareCentrix and Summit Health which were not included in
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, and higher investments in the organic business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss was $472&nbsp;million. Adjusted
operating loss was $159&nbsp;million, which excludes certain costs related to stock compensation, amortization of acquired intangible assets, and acquisition related costs. Adjusted EBITDA loss was $109&nbsp;million, reflecting VillageMD expansion
and higher organic business investments, partly offset by positive contributions from Shields and CareCentrix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA will hold a conference call to discuss the second quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, March&nbsp;28, 2023. A live simulcast as well as
related presentation materials will be available through WBA&#146;s investor relations website at: https://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A replay of the conference will be archived on the website for at least 12 months after the event. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">*All references to net earnings or net loss are to net earnings or net loss attributable to WBA, and all references to EPS are to diluted EPS attributable to WBA. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">**&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow amounts are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the
appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely correlated GAAP measure. The Company defines Adjusted EBITDA as segment operating
income/(loss) before depreciation, amortization, and stock-based compensation; in addition to these items, the Company excludes certain other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments, when they occur, as further defined. </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:13pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an
integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 13,000 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the
healthcare ecosystem. The Company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its purpose &#150; to create more joyful lives through better health. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of health
services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA employs more than 325,000 people and has a presence in nine countries through its portfolio of consumer brands: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the No7 Beauty
Company, Benavides in Mexico and Ahumada in Chile. Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including China and the U.S. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA has been recognized for
its commitment to operating sustainably: the Company is an index component of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI) and was named to the 100 Best Corporate Citizens 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">More Company information is available at www.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:80pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(WBA-ER)</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules,
presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The Company has provided the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and
presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has
evaluated the Company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the Company&#146;s historical operating results. These
supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented
in the press release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis where
it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various
items that have not yet occurred, are out of the Company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, such as unusual <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> charges, tax expenses, and material litigation expenses, and that would
impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company also presents certain information related to
current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange
rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The Company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the U.S. transacting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this
presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least
twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster, in the past twelve months as well as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable sales for the
first twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable
retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the Company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same
as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented
on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">10 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company considers certain metrics, such as comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions, comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, number of payor/ provider partnerships, number of locations of Walgreens Health Corners, number of VillageMD <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-located</FONT> clinics and number of
total VillageMD/Summit/CityMD locations, at period end, to be key performance indicators because the Company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented
provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as
a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the total number of VillageMD locations, locations are defined as the primary care locations where the Company or the Company&#146;s affiliates lease or
license space and the providers are employed by either the Company or one of the Company&#146;s affiliates. These locations are primarily branded as Village Medical where the Company employs the providers but, in some instances, may operate under
their own brands. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">12 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain legal
proceedings, including legal defense costs. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of
the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. During the three and six months ended February&nbsp;28, 2023, the Company recorded charges related to the previously announced
opioid litigation settlement frameworks and certain other opioid-related matters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory valuation
adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and
contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated
by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an
intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment
reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree
awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These charges are
primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include charges incurred related to certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in operating income, for example, costs related to integration efforts for merger, acquisition
and divestitures activities. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock compensation and employee transaction success bonuses. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are
significantly impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for
using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices,
which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on the sale of equity method investments. During the three and six months ended
February&nbsp;28, 2023, the Company recorded a gain of $492&nbsp;million and $1.5&nbsp;billion, respectively, in Other income (expense), net, due to a partial sale of its equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">8</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in foreign
subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within Other income (expense), net. We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying
derivative instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">9</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of equity method investment and investment in equity securities includes impairment of certain investments. The
Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business and it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis. Exclusion of such charges enables more
consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Other income (expense), net. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">10</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on business combinations due to the remeasurement of previously held minority equity interests
and debt securities to fair value. During the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2021, the Company recorded such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gains of $2.2&nbsp;billion and $402&nbsp;million for VillageMD and Shields,
respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">11</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">During the three months ended February&nbsp;28, 2022, the Company finalized the working capital adjustments with
AmerisourceBergen related to the sale of the Alliance Healthcare business, resulting in a $38&nbsp;million charge recorded to Other income (expense), net in the Consolidated Condensed Statement of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">12</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision (benefit) include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax (benefit) provision commensurate
with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. and UK tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income
tax provision (benefit). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">13</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">post-tax</FONT> earnings from other equity method investments consist of
the proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments.
These charges are recorded within <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">post-tax</FONT> earnings from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in
these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">14</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from the reported net loss, the impact of potentially dilutive securities on the
per share amounts has been omitted from the calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted EPS for the six months ended February&nbsp;28, 2023. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

adjusted diluted net earnings per common share calculation purposes. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company reconciles Adjusted EBITDA for the U.S. Healthcare segment to Operating loss as the closest GAAP measure for
the segment profitability. The Company does not measure Net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. for its segments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory valuation
adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and
contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated
by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an
intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment
reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree
awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include charges incurred related to certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in operating income, for example, costs related to integration efforts for merger, acquisition
and divestitures activities. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock compensation and employee transaction success bonuses. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are
significantly impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes GAAP stock-based compensation expense excluding expenses related to acquisition-related amortization and
acquisition-related costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures), plus acquisition related payments made in that period. This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt
service and other contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">During the three months ended February&nbsp;28, 2023, the Company paid $335&nbsp;million to settle liability classified
share-based payment awards related to acquiring the remaining 30% equity interest in Shields. The Company also paid <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> compensation costs related to VillageMD&#146;s acquisition of Summit. The payments
are not indicative of normal operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
